WHEN IS A QUINCUNX GOOD OR BAD?
(With reference to Post 483 and some emails from other members.)
A number of our members have informed us that when it comes to Electional Astrology
and the choosing of propitious dates to commence an endeavor, they are having
difficulty understanding how Magi Astrology deals with this issue.
We are writing this post as a teaching guide.
To begin with, a quincunx occurs whenever two planets are aligned at 150 degrees (plus
or minus the usual Magi orb). The quincunx aspect is the most complicated of angles to
evaluate because the influence has a wider range of valid interpretations than any other
class of aspect. The quincunx is so complex that before the Magi Society, astrologers
generally ignored it because they did not know what to make of it.
To help guide our members, we have below written a summary of how to judge
whether a quincunx is helpful or otherwise for the purposes of Electional Astrology.
But we must begin by introducing some new terminology –

WITHOUT MALEFIC
The first is WITHOUT MALEFIC. If an aspect is WITHOUT MALEFIC, it means the
aspect is formed by two planets and neither of them is Saturn. In Magi Astrology, Saturn
is the only malefic. When we say an aspect is formed without malefic, it means that
neither of the two planets that form the aspect is Saturn.

WITH MALEFIC
Obviously if an aspect is formed WITH MALEFIC, this would mean that the aspect is
formed by Saturn and another planet.

306

WITH BENEFIC
We also need to discuss what we mean by the term WITH BENEFIC. In Magi Astrology,
we consider Jupiter as the only benefic. An aspect that is formed with benefic is one that
is formed by Jupiter and another planet.
Armed with this additional terminology, we are now ready to present the Magi
Astrology rules for evaluating a quincunx for Electional Astrology (please remember
that in our third book, we explained that when it comes to Personal Aspects, all natal
aspects are heavenly gifts of a special talent; but this is not the case with Electional
Astrology or anything outside of Personal Astrology):

For Electional Astrology
A) For Electional Astrology, you should normally avoid choosing a day with any
quincunx that is with malefic. In other words, it is risky to natalize anything when there
is a quincunx formed by Saturn and any other planet. However, there are exceptions to
this rule. We explained some of the exceptions in the last part of Lesson Three of our
Members Only Website. In that lesson, we taught that an elected chart couldn't be
successful if there is PERSONALITY MISMATCH. For example, if you are choosing a
date for the release of a movie or book about tragic loss of life (like the movie Titanic),
you must include an aspect that represents loss of life. The best aspect to represent loss
of life is the Saturn-Chiron quincunx. That is an aspect that the Titanic movie had when
it was released to the public.
But it should be obvious that if you are starting a new corporation and it is going to be a
drug company, you would not want the Saturn-Chiron quincunx in the chart. (As you
can see, you REALLY need to KNOW what you are doing when selecting an Electional
Chart.)
B) All quincunx aspects formed without malefic are enhancement aspects! In other
words, it is helpful to natalize days when a quincunx is formed by two planets and
neither of the planets is Saturn. But there are complexities to this rule. If you wish to
fully master Electional Astrology, you have to understand the differences between the
three different types of quincunxes.
Double Retrograde quincunx
1. The Double Retrograde quincunx is both powerful and helpful for an elected chart.
Two retrograde planets form such a quincunx.
A bi-directional quincunx
2. A bi-directional quincunx (where one planet is in retrograde while the other is in
direct motion) is also very helpful but a little less powerful.
Double Direct quincunx
3. There is a third type of quincunx. It is the Double Direct quincunx where both planets
are in direct motion. A Double Direct quincunx is a two-edged sword and unless you

307

have fully mastered Magi Astrology, it is better to avoid them in an elected chart. The
reason is that a Double Direct quincunx, especially if close to exact, is sometimes TOO
powerful and it can overwhelm the other aspects and can therefore be DISRUPTIVE. For
example, if a corporation is formed with a Venus-Uranus Double Direct quincunx, the
desire (Venus) for change (Uranus) might be so overpowering that the corporation could
never have the tenacity to finish a major project. That would be disruptive. (However it
would be a great natal aspect for a company that owns amusement parks with wild
rides like looping roller coasters because Uranus rules excitement, so Venus-Uranus
quincunx would represent overpowering desire for excitement.)
However, if a corporation were founded during a bi-directional or double retrograde
quincunx of Venus-Uranus, rather than a double direct one, it would always be good
because such an aspect would provide the help of Venus-Uranus aspects, but without
the destabilizing influence of the Double Direct aspect.

not good to be married during a Double Direct quincunx of Mars-Pluto
As another example, it is not good to be married during a Double Direct quincunx of
Mars-Pluto because the marriage could be too oriented towards sex and might not allow
the attainment of everything else needed to make a marriage happy and lifelong. The
desire for sex could be overpowering and would disrupt the marriage.
However, a bi-directional or double-retrograde quincunx of Mars and Pluto would be
very good in a Marriage Chart because it adds enough spice without being
overpowering and without the single-minded passion that would detract from the rest
of the marriage.
So when is a Double Direct quincunx good? It depends on a lot of factors and our point
is that the Double Direct quincunx is too complex for the novice astrologer to play with.
It is too powerful to include in an Electional chart unless you know exactly what you are
doing and have truly mastered Magi Astrology.
Our third book was written with the idea that our readers have not yet mastered Magi
Astrology. For this reason, we wrote that if you are choosing a date for a marriage or a
job, you should not ever choose a date with a Double Direct quincunx. That is the safe
rule of thumb. We wrote this because we did not want to have to go into all the details
that we are now writing about. (After all, our third book was for beginners; we had to
write for beginners because that is what the publisher wanted.)
(On page 232, the third book said, "Double Direct quincunxes are Turbulent Aspects."
That was a typo due to a mistake by the publisher. It should have read "Double Direct
quincunxes are turbulent aspects" meaning they are disruptive. But they are not
Turbulent Aspects like Clashes.)
At the Magi Society, we natalize charts with Double Direct quincunxes all the time. We
like to think we have mastered Magi Astrology so we know when we should, and when
we should not, natalize them.
There is another wrinkle in all this. It happens that when a Double Direct quincunx is
With Benefic, then the aspect is not disruptive. A Double Direct quincunx that is formed
by Jupiter and another planet (except Saturn) is very helpful and provides just the right

308

amount of power. The presence of Jupiter makes the aspect stabilizing rather than
disruptive. This is because Jupiter is so good.
Our final point for this post is:
The upcoming Jupiter-Pluto quincunx is very helpful because it is with benefic and we
recommend that you take advantage of it.
(We know that some of you will wonder why we made this post during a Sun-Saturn
square. For one thing, Saturn is not applying to the Sun so there is no Saturn to Sun
progression or transit. For another reason, the Chiron-Neptune midpoint is trine the
Sun. Venus trines Pluto and is contra-parallel Chiron. And we have some other very
good reasons that we will teach later.)

Aug. 16, 2001
I noticed one of today’s headlines: TECH WOES ON WALL STREET, subtitled: ‘Tech
stocks tumble in early trading based on forecast..." I remembered that Saturn had been
opposed to Pluto for some time which could indicate a constricting of big business in
general, but ‘Tech' stocks would seem to need Uranus in the mix somehow and the last I
looked there was no such aspect.
Curious, I cast a chart for the day and was astounded, but not altogether surprised to see
the Sun Opposite Uranus; a bad day for high technology values. The Saturn opposition
to Pluto is separating and peaked 10 days ago but is still in “orb.” So it seems that the
Saturn “fallout” would be lurking and the Sun-Uranus opposition (applying yesterday)
would bring the cumulative effect home to roost on Wall Street.
In the Declinations, Venus//Saturn and applying for 6 days at .86 degree orb, very tight
but not quite Magical Time of influence — a constricting (Saturn) of the flow of money
(Venus). I wondered why Wall Street reacted so skittishly to a fairy weak forecast by
some agency. It is then I noticed an amazing thing. In the declinations for today Mercury
was virtually EXACT to Pluto at .01 degrees and applying for a mere 27 minutes at the
time of the announcement of the so-called forecast. But how would that matter? It would
seem to me that the damaging forecast was percipitated by NEWS (Mercury) of big
business (Pluto). Altogether, the news was not so good. But there’s more.

324

Now I was really curious. I quickly cast a chart for a look at the Heliocentric Sky and to
my amazement there was a T-Square comprised of Chiron Opposite Jupiter both square
to, guess what? Mercury. The T-Square dissipated rather quickly but the forecast was let
loose during that time. Most of the critical aspects happened yesterday (Aug 15) and I
guess that is the reason for the “Early Morning Tumble” as soon as the stock market
opened.
Other Helio aspects of note: The Earth/Moon complex is applying to a Square to Venus
close to Magical time of 3.6 days today joined by, guess who? Uranus conjunct the
Earth/Moon complex forming a conjuncted square: A bad day (square) for money
(Venus) in technology stocks (Uranus) affecting world markets (Earth/Moon Complex).
The more we learn about Magi astrology, the more empowered we are to see clearly and
accurately how astrology really works.
Sincerely,
jjf

This is in response to some statements made by JJF in post 424
In your post you state:
*******************************************
Well, we all know traditional astrology has jumped through hoops to
try to explain such enigmas with the calculated points of
ascendencies, midheavens, etc. But the Magi have conclusive proof that
none of those techniques are statistically valid.
**********************************************
This statement echos to the statement in post 420 that you
made with regard to being confused as to precisely what the Magi had
proven in Astrology Really Works ( or throughout the rest of their
work for that matter) It may help you to
re-read the material that the Magi have
written. The Magi have stated that they have no statistical
verification of the usefulness of any house system...HOWEVER, they
have not ever made any statement with regard to the calculated points,
the Ascendant and the Midheaven being statistically invalid at
all.........the Magi did not enter Ascendant or Midheaven data into
some of their statistical studies because this data is time sensitive,
ie requires that one has a correct birthtime within 4 minutes of being
exact. The Magi expressly stated that in setting up the statistical
research which they released a portion of in Astrology Really Works,
they determined to avoid the issue of exact birth times one, because
exact birthtimes are very hard to come by, much harder to come by than
an accurate birthdate, and more importantly because debunkers and
skeptics ordinarily use this as a point of dispute in an attempt to
disprove any other findings...ie, the debunkers challenge that the
birth times in the data set were incorrect...which then invalidates
all findings. The Magi, being very very wise, took that potential
argument out of the debunkers hands altogether by stating “we don’t
even need to look at birth times to do a very valid statistical study
which is reliant only on measuring the alignments of planets to one
another”.

326

However, there is a world of difference between not having this
information confirmed via one particular statistical study or group of
studies undertaken for one express purpose and stating that this
information is ‘invalid’. Far from it, the Magi have routinely
mentioned exactly the opposite. Let’s look at one obvious example.
In Astrology Really Works , on page 127, in discussing the negative
ruling progression that Ron Goldman had of Saturn quincunx Uranus
which peaked when he was 25, the year he was murdered by ‘someone’,
the Magi then state:
“Please do not have nightmares if you find that you or a loved one has
the same progression. It is a very tough progression, but there is no
progression so bad that it cannot be overcome, especially if you are
forewarned of it. We are certain that in Goldman’s case, he had very
strong negatives to his calculated points, such as the midheaven and
ascendant, (my stress added) as well as other negative progressions to
his natal planets. “
That certainly doesn’t sound as though the Magi Authors are
considering the calculated points of midheaven and ascendant as being
‘invalid’ in any way now does it?

rather large lists of planetary symbolisms for us. But when we look at
a chart of someone we do not know, WE have to expand our view, not
contract it.
In analyzing a Natal chart, we have to look at ALL the symbolic
meanings as potential manifestations.

Golden Rectangle was formed in the CAC
In looking at the couple that Corey mentioned in post 413 a
Golden Rectangle was formed in the CAC of the two people..
recently I took some time to set down the following to
explain a Golden Rectangle to another party...some of the
readers of the board might find it a mildly useful diversion, so
I'll share it with you in case it might be helpful.
Let's also consider something particularly interesting with regard to
a Golden Rectangle...while it does not have the completely symmetrical
midpoint support of a Grand Trine ( wherein not only is Element A
enhanced by element B and C, but is likewise enhanced specifically by
the midpoint of the exact same pair...same for B with A and C, and C
with A and B)...but the Golden Rectangle still comes in with
significant internal geometric support. Remember that each Golden
rectangle is formed by two trines and two sextiles, and two
oppositions....but that what we also have within a Golden Rectangle
are Two Magi Quads...the definition of a Magi Quad in longitude being
conjuncted/opposed midpoint pairings ( opposition due to the Law of
Midpoint Projection...ie with regard to Midpoints, there always being
both a near and far midpoint, anytime one sees an opposition to the
midpoint one understands a conjunction to the midpoint as well). Due
to the structure of a Golden Rectangle, all four of the elements in
the rectangle are enhanced by midpoints of two of the other elements

328

belonging to the other long side. With a Quad consisting of Trine A to
B, and Trine C to D, with A sextile D and B sextile C, A/B trines C,
A/B trines D, and C/D trines A , C/D trines B. In addition, we have
A/B conjunct C/D ( A+BC+D) and A/D conjunct B/C ( A+DB+C).
A --------------A/B-------------B
|\/\/|
|\/|
A/C / \ B/D
|\/
/\/\|
C-------------- C/D-------------D
Where we have a bit of a lack of symmetry is that A/C doesn't enhance
any of the specific individual elements, nor does B/D...where as in a
Grand Trine we have this overlapping and re-combining of all of the
elements in enhancement alignment....and we also have two oppositions.
Two Trines, 4 enhancements by midpoints, 2 quads...and two
oppositions. In a certain sense , without considering the specific
trines or oppositions involved, we can understand the two trines and
two oppositions as 'balancing' against each other...a net 0 within the
configuration alone (do not confuse my statement here with what is
written in the manuals with regard to tallying interp ratings...this
has nothing whatsoever do do with this..what I am exploring here is
the relative effectiveness of all of the disparate elements which
combine to form this unique structure)...but the significant double
quadrature and quadruple midpoint enhancements add the significant
power. With regard to a Golden Rectangle, being more specific,
depending upon which unique elements are involved, the different
trines and oppositions can have significantly different power
individually...in one we may have a Jupiter trine to Chiron, or Venus
trine to Chiron...while in another we might have Saturn opposite
Chiron or Saturn opposite Jupiter. Considering the individual power of
the trines and oppositions which contribute to the formation of the
configuration allows for greater understanding.

between two persons. Declinational midpoints seem to be slightly more

midpoint enhances someone else’s Mars, that person will be much more
likely to have a sexual attraction to you. But if your Saturn/Pluto
midpoint aspects someone’s Mars, you do not have much of a chance.
This is all a part of what everyone has been calling ‘chemistry’. It
really is in the stars!”

This is the conclusion of part III of our Magi analysis of the fraternal twins enigma. As
stated in our previous post #431, the purpose was to see how such different lives could be
explained by our Magi studies. Twin A is a Presbyterian Minister and Twin B is a Software
Consultant. So let us take a look at the significant Magi aspects that the twins share.
A. The first thing we notice is a JUPITER-URANUS PLANETARY ECLIPSE. This is a very
powerful superfame aspect involving the public, high technology, politics, entertainment
etc. The logitudinal orb is very tight as is the declinational, withing .2 degrees.
1. We can see that both the twins are deeply involved in and successful at dealing with the
public, Twin A as a minister and Twin B as a computer genius. Each of these careers fit
within the Magi planetary symbolism. Both twins are successful in their fields and held in
high esteem by masses of people through the use of their Jupiter/Uranian talents (eclipse).
2. We determined that the eclipse was powerful enough to allow for a slightly wider orb
that reveals a square to Neptune which, in a natal chart, symbolizes intense focus of
SCIENTIFIC
AND
RELIGIOUS
matters.
3. The Jupiter-Uranus conjunction is also trine Saturn. Thus we have the “Fallen Angel”
aspect. Indeed, Twin B rebelled in the early years against the prevailing mores using the
Saturn-Jupiter aspect, while Twin A manifested the influence of the Saturn-Uranus (control
of the public mind through his ministry).
B. They have another Super Aspect of Jupiter//Pluto, success in big business. Obviously
software consulting for large firms and one of the biggest religious organizations in the
world fit the twins seeming enigma of different lives. We will not go into such detail for all
the aspects, but you get the picture of what we are seeking to understand through our
Magi work. As you review the following Multiple Planet Aspects, keep in mind also that
BOTH the twins are accomplished musicians.

Well, those are some highlights from our study. It became clear that the enigma of the
twins was only a surface phenomena and in no way did their manifested careers deviate
from the principles and symbolism of Magi astrology. In fact, without the power of Magi
Multiple Planet Aspects including MDX’s and Magi Quads, their lives may have forever
remained an enigma to us.
The study of the twins gave us a new appreciation for the expanded Magi symbolism and
the cutting edge techniques of Magi geometry. Together with the Magi Principles stated in
our previous posts, we can now look at a Natal chart and see the range of potentials
available to the incarnating soul under a given set of stars and be more accurate than ever
in our evaluations. All of this served to further strengthen and deepen our belief that
astrology really does work.

Twins
This is Part III of three of our Green Team’s excursion into the questions raised regarding
people with the same stars who manifest seemingly different lives. Initially, our subject
opened with questions about the chart of such a one as Hitler (post #412). In that study,
the Magi Principle of Benevolent Design came to the fore, showing us that a Natal chart
does not predict the choices the soul makes on its journey through this lifetime, but the
soul, indeed, has choices it must make and must be responsible for.
Our second question centered around a team member who had the same chart as a
famous actress, yet was not famous (post #424). However, we found many similarities in
the actual lives of these two souls. Again, with our previous principle of Divine
Benevolence as our base of wisdom, we began to see how the Magi principle of Fraternal
Symbolism helped us expand our understanding. We learned that the new, expanded
Magi symbolism of the planets gave us the tools we needed to see how seemingly
dissimilar lives actually fit very nicely within the range of Magi interpretations and, in fact
proved that such lives were not so dissimilar after all.
I thought we had put this study to rest until I received another letter from Merilyn who had
one more example that seemed to defy our astrological comprehension. The new subject

337

for consideration was a very old enigma that many astrologers question and ponder; the
dreaded enigma of the fraternal twins!
Through two of our members, our team had the good fortune to know of such twins
personally. Their lives were utterly different. Or so it seemed. One grew up to be a
Presbyterian minister and we refer to him as Twin A. The other one grew up to be a
musician, computer genius, writer and a crusader for freedom and we refer to him as Twin
B. If you would like to cast a chart, the twins were born on January 24, 1955.
Traditional astrology is certainly not lacking in theories to tackle such enigmas and many
of them are, no doubt, correct. Past life experiences are one such explanation. I have
never met an astrologer who did not try to factor in Reincarnation. But we are students of
Magi Astrology and the material we currently have before us does not specifically address
this mystery. However, we agreed that we would attempt to probe the Twins enigma using
only the tools offered to us thus far in our Magi studies. As it turned out, we had more tools
than we at first thought.
Initially, we were trapped in the mindset of “different lives.” As we pondered this, it
occurred to me that we should focus, instead on what the Twins had in common. We
began to apply the full set of Magi Planetary symbolism, the principle of Fraternal
symbolism and the principle of Planetary Transformation. We ignored what we knew about
the Twins and analyzed the chart with an open view, a chart without a name and without a
known history. We began to collect our data and build, as it were, a profile of potential
manifestations that anyone born on that day might have as their spectrum of potentialities
within the Magi planetary symbolism.
And again, we were amazed at how much the twins really had in common and how they
each used the same set of talents to fashion unique lives. Magi astrology proved to be our
search light into the vast complexities of life. Some of our technical analysis will follow in
another post.

CERTIFICATION CANDIDATES
The Magi Society Board of Governors has decided to make the Certification Program
more flexible and valuable and will be instituting some changes to the program.
We have decided to divide the Certification Program into four stages. To complete each
stage, a Candidate must produce an acceptable paper and pass a test. When a
Candidate successfully completes each stage, the Candidate will be given a title and a
certificate. The four titles associated with the completion of each stage are:
Stage One: Magi Instructor
Stage Two: Assistant Magi (Asst. Magi)
Stage Three: Associate Magi (Assoc. Magi)

338

Stage Four: Certified Magi Astrologer (CMA)
By making the above changes, a Candidate will no longer have to complete the entire
18-month Certification program before being able to be accredited by the Magi Society
to practice and charge for astrological consultations using Magi Astrology. Even a Magi
Instructor will be sanctioned and authorized by the Magi Society to charge clients for
Magi Astrology Consultations.
We will provide complete details of the requirements of the four stages in early October.
In the meantime, we suggest that all Candidates complete their Foundation Papers by
then.

Marilyn Monroe's birth year as 1927. This is not correct. It should have been 1926. All
Certification Candidates should make note of this fact and make the appropriate
correction. We apologize for any inconvenience this error may have caused. We thank
the members who brought this mistake to our attention.)

fascinated with Financial Astrology.

include a section where you apply the principles of Magi Astrology to each of the
celebrity couples to explain the relationship each couple has (or had).

may do whatever you like in the paper but you must include a section where you apply

corporations were able to be so successful in their particular type(s) of business that they
were successful in.

principles of Magi Astrology and using famous examples to illustrate these principles.

software manuals.

has been approved, you may substitute that topic for the choices above.
